country_event = { #The Year of the Rat
	id = CHI.introgame.003
	title = CHI.introgame.003.t
	desc = CHI.introgame.003.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_china_abandoned

	is_triggered_only = yes  #Fired 3 days after 1.1.1936

	option = { #Court the League of Ten
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.introgame.003 option CHI.introgame.003.a"
		name = CHI.introgame.003.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.01 }
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_minor_events_tt
	}
	option = { #Court the OCC liberals
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.introgame.003 option CHI.introgame.003.b"
		name = CHI.introgame.003.b
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.01 }
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_minor_events_tt
	}
	option = { #Court the LCS
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.introgame.003 option CHI.introgame.003.c"
		name = CHI.introgame.003.c
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.01 }
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_minor_events_tt
	}
}

country_event = { #The Harvest of 1936
	id = CHI.earlygame.001
	title = CHI.earlygame.001.t
	desc = CHI.earlygame.001.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_economic

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by CHI.earlygame.000, should be on June 24th, 1936

	option = { #They'll have to get used to these changes for the greater good.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.earlygame.001 option CHI.earlygame.001.a"
		name = CHI.earlygame.001.a
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_command_power = 30
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -40
	}

	option = { #Divert new recruits to get some moral training in the fields.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.earlygame.001 option CHI.earlygame.001.b"
		name = CHI.earlygame.001.b
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_manpower = -100000 #You have around 130k after you secure your cores during League War
		army_experience = -30
		add_war_support = 0.10
	}
}

country_event = { #The Secretive Retainer
	id = CHI.earlygame.002
	title = CHI.earlygame.002.t
	desc = CHI.earlygame.002.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_intelligence

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event lepcollapse.19

	option = { #Is that so?
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.earlygame.002 option CHI.earlygame.002.a"
		name = CHI.earlygame.002.a
		add_intel = {
			target = CHI
			civilian_intel = 10
			army_intel = 15
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_dai_chunfeng_advisor
		set_country_flag = CHI_dai_li_recruited_lep_flag
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_dai_chunfeng = { set_nationality = LEP }
			promote_character = {
				character = CHI_dai_chunfeng
				ideology = totalist_subtype
			}
			CHI = {
				country_event = { id = CHI.earlygame.003 days = 3 } #Spies and Secrets in the League War
			}
		}
	}
}

###- Early Game Events Triggered By On-Actions (200-299) -###

country_event = { # Return of the Central Committee - fired by completing capture of Xiamen
	id = CHI.earlygame.200
	title = CHI.earlygame.200.t
	desc = CHI.earlygame.200.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_wang_jingwei_plane_takeoff

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.earlygame.200 option CHI.earlygame.200.a"
		name = CHI.earlygame.200.a
		division_template = {
			name = "Dúli Bubing Lü"    # Represents: small professional units for early 2nd NRA
			division_names_group = CHI_INF_04
			regiments = {
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 } # Note: Chinese divisions were brigade-sized compared to other nations' armies
				infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 } # Lit. 'Independent Infantry Brigade' in Mandarin (tone inconsistencies match HOI4 Vanilla)
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
				infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
			}
		}
		division_template = {

		CHI_LCS_shatter_flag_effect = yes
		set_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.midgame.028 option CHI.midgame.028.a"
		name = CHI.midgame.028.a #A return to the status quo.
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag }
			CHI_LCS_small_effect = yes
			CHI_PAC_small_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag }
			CHI_LCS_small_effect = yes
			CHI_RCA_small_effect = yes
		}
		else = {
			CHI_LCS_medium_effect = yes
		}
		CHI_sub_rad_small_effect = yes
		promote_character = {
			character = CHI_chen_duxiu
			ideology = syndicalist_subtype
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				name = CHI_csp_ort_party
				long_name = CHI_csp_ort_party_long
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Fired from Eyes in the Dark Focus
	id = CHI.midgame.208
	title = CHI.midgame.208.t
	desc = CHI.midgame.208.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_cardgame

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Empower Zhou Enlai's Teke
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.midgame.208 option CHI.midgame.208.a"
		name = CHI.midgame.208.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_RCA_victory = yes
			}
		}
		CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CHI_chose_teke_flag
			country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.209 days = 1 random_days = 1 } #Heroics of Teke
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_zhou_enlai
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_lar = no }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = CHI_teke_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_intelligence_agency = no }
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_form_department } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_form_department
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_psycho_warfare } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_psycho_warfare
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 50 }
	}
	option = { #Empower Dai's BIS
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.midgame.208 option CHI.midgame.208.b"
		name = CHI.midgame.208.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_hu_victory = yes
			}
		}
		CHI_CRS_large_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CHI_chose_bis_flag
			country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.210 days = 1 random_days = 1 } #The BIS on the march!
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_dai_chunfeng_advisor
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_lar = no }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = CHI_bis_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_intelligence_agency = no }
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_army_department } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_army_department
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_invisible_ink } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_invisible_ink
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 50 }
	}
	option = { #Combine both - form the Ministry of State Security (MSS)
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.midgame.208 option CHI.midgame.208.c"
		name = CHI.midgame.208.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_song_victory = yes
			}
		}
		CHI_CRS_small_effect = yes
		CHI_RCA_small_effect = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = CHI_chose_mss_flag
			country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.212 days = 180 random_days = 10 } #Dysfunction in the MSS
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
		show_ideas_tooltip = CHI_dai_chunfeng_advisor
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc_lar = no }
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = CHI_mss_idea
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_intelligence_agency = no }
			create_intelligence_agency = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_commando_training } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_commando_training
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_done_agency_upgrade = upgrade_passive_defense } }
			upgrade_intelligence_agency = upgrade_passive_defense
		}
		else = { add_political_power = 50 }
	}

		}

	major = yes

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.midgame.211 option CHI.midgame.211.a"

			NOT = { tag = CHI }

		}
		if = {

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = HNN }
			CHI = { CHI_tang_zong = { set_nationality = HNN promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = LEC }
			CHI = { CHI_shen_zui = { set_nationality = LEC promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = QIE }
			CHI = { CHI_ma_hansan = { set_nationality = QIE promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = SHX } #SHX's leader is already in SHX
			effect_tooltip = { SHX_qiao_jiacai = { set_nationality = SHX promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = SQI }
			CHI = { CHI_hu_tianqiu = { set_nationality = SQI promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = SZC }
			CHI = { CHI_zeng_kuoqing = { set_nationality = SZC promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = YUN }
			CHI = { CHI_qiu_kaiji = { set_nationality = YUN promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}

		}
		CHI_CRS_small_effect = yes
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.midgame.211 option CHI.midgame.211.a"
		name = CHI.midgame.211.a

			NOT = { tag = CHI }
			CHI = { has_country_flag = CHI_chose_teke_flag }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {

					tag = TIB
					tag = MON
				}
			}

				long_name = CHI_totalist_teke_generic_long
				name = CHI_totalist_teke_generic
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { original_tag = FNG }
			CHI = { CHI_yan_baohang = { set_nationality = FNG promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = GXC }
			CHI = { CHI_gong_changrong = { set_nationality = GXC promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = HNN }
			CHI = { CHI_liu_daoheng = { set_nationality = HNN promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = LEC }
			CHI = { CHI_tan_zhongyu = { set_nationality = LEC promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = QIE }
			CHI = { CHI_wang_shijian = { set_nationality = QIE promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = SHX } #SHX's leader is already in SHX
			SHX_bo_yibo = {
				add_country_leader_role = { country_leader = { ideology = totalist_subtype } }
				promote_character = totalist_subtype
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = SQI }
			CHI = { CHI_kang_sheng = { set_nationality = SQI promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = SZC }
			CHI = { CHI_hu_chunpu = { set_nationality = SZC promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = XSM }
			CHI = { CHI_wu_hongbin = { set_nationality = XSM promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { original_tag = YUN } #YUN's leader is already in SHX
			effect_tooltip = { YUN_wang_fusheng = { set_nationality = YUN promote_character = totalist_subtype } }
		}
	}
	option = { #Courageous men in dire times.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.midgame.211 option CHI.midgame.211.d"
		name = CHI.midgame.211.d
		trigger = {
			original_tag = CHI
			has_country_flag = CHI_chose_teke_flag
		}
		CHI_RCA_small_effect = yes
	}
}

		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM.FROM = { china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes } }
			add_political_power = -35 #How dare they???
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { FROM.FROM = { china_is_aligned_with_republicans = yes } }
			add_political_power = -25 #How dare they???
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -10
		}
	}
}

#Outside Negotiation Events

country_event = { #A Republican Pact?
	id = CHI.midgame.901
	title = CHI.midgame.901.t
	desc = CHI.midgame.901.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_GXC_federalist_party_3
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by decision CHI_NAP_with_federalists_decision
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = CHI }
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.midgame.901 option CHI.midgame.901.a"
		name = CHI.midgame.901.a #The corrupt Beiyang warlords must fall! We accept.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Feds don't want multiple wars
				factor = 3
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = { #If the political situation in China has drastically changed
				factor = 5
				OR = {
					QIE = { exists = no }
					FNG = { exists = no }
					any_other_country = {
						is_chinese_tag = yes
						has_war_with = JAP
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CHI = { CHI_gu_mengyu = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			}
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FROM
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { CHI = { CHI_gu_mengyu = { is_second_in_command = yes } } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -40
		}
		set_country_flag = CHI_UPC_NAP_flag
		FROM = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.902 days = 3 } } } #[FROM.GetNameDefCap] Accepts Our Pact!
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.midgame.901 option CHI.midgame.901.b"
		name = CHI.midgame.901.b #The Kuomintang are little better than red tyrants.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.3
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 2
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Feds less likely to agree if KMT is choking them
				factor = 3
				all_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						tag = FROM
						is_subject_of = FROM
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure # of Fed Puppets
				factor = 5
				num_subjects > 4
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CHI_ally_betrayal option = CHI_ALLY_BETRAYAL_NEVER }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_hates_govt
		}
		FROM = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.midgame.903 days = 3 } } } #[FROM.GetNameDefCap] Rejects Our Pact!
	}
}

country_event = { #Xu Qian Passes Away
	id = CHI.lategame.040
	title = CHI.lategame.040.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.040.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { CHI_is_phase_four_trigger = no } #Make sure powerstruggle is still active
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random = {
				chance = 50
				set_country_flag = CHI_nar_rev_ord_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_nar_rev_ord_flag }
				country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.050 days = 180 random_days = 10 } #Liu Shaoqi in Fujian
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.041 days = 180 random_days = 10 } #The Chen Bijun Incident!
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.040.a #Cai Yuanpei is a steady choice.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.040 option CHI.lategame.040.a"
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_song_victory = yes
			}
		}
		CHI_PAC_small_effect = yes
		CHI_WRD_SOC_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.040.b #Luo Junqiang to send a message.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.040 option CHI.lategame.040.b"

				country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.048 days = 180 random_days = 10 } #The Shifting Underground
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.050 days = 180 random_days = 10 } #Liu Shaoqi in Fujian
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.049.a #The Father and Son of a New China!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.049 option CHI.lategame.049.a"
		ai_chance = {

			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_wang_victory = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_RCA_victory = yes
			}
		}
		CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = CHI.lategame.049.b #His actual son would like a word...
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.049 option CHI.lategame.049.b"
		ai_chance = {

				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_song_victory = yes
			}
		}
		CHI_RF_medium_effect = yes
	}

	title = CHI.lategame.201.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.201.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_wang_jingwei_speech_preparation

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus CHI_third_national_congress
	timeout_days = 7
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { CHI_wang_jingwei = { has_trait = CHI_emergency_powers } }
				CHI_wang_jingwei = { remove_trait = { trait = CHI_emergency_powers ideology = radical_socialist_subtype } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Destiny Beckons
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.201 option CHI.lategame.201.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.201.a
		effect_tooltip = { remove_ideas = CHI_calls_for_congress_idea }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_convention_called_tt
	}
}

country_event = { #A League Divided
	id = CHI.lategame.207
	title = CHI.lategame.207.t
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.207.d.LCS
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = LCS_shattered_flag } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.207.d.ORT
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.207.d.RAD
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_RAD_dom_flag }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.207.d.WRD
		trigger = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_WRD_dom_flag }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_worker

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus CHI_third_national_congress
	timeout_days = 7

	option = { #We stand against reactionary subversion!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.207 option CHI.lategame.207.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.207.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_WRD_dom_flag
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag
					has_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_lcs_divided_rca_tt
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = LCS_shattered_flag } }
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.05 }
				CHI_RCA_mega_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.03 }
				CHI_RCA_large_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.01 }
				CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				CHI_RCA_small_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
						has_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag }
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.15 }
				CHI_RCA_mega_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.10 }
				CHI_RCA_large_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.05 }
				CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				CHI_RCA_small_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
						has_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.30 }
				CHI_RCA_mega_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.20 }
				CHI_RCA_large_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.10 }
				CHI_RCA_medium_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				CHI_RCA_small_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Wang has become too much of a danger!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.207 option CHI.lategame.207.b"
		name = CHI.lategame.207.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_RAD_dom_flag
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag
					has_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_lcs_divided_pac_tt
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = LCS_shattered_flag } }
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.05 }
				CHI_PAC_mega_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.03 }
				CHI_PAC_large_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.01 }
				CHI_PAC_medium_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				CHI_PAC_small_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
						has_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag }
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.15 }
				CHI_PAC_mega_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.10 }
				CHI_PAC_large_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.05 }
				CHI_PAC_medium_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				CHI_PAC_small_effect = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
						has_country_flag = CHI_rca_lcs_alignment_flag
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = CHI_pac_lcs_alignment_flag
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.30 }
				CHI_PAC_mega_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.20 }
				CHI_PAC_large_effect = yes
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { syndicalist > 0.10 }
				CHI_PAC_medium_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				CHI_PAC_small_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Liberals Push On
	id = CHI.lategame.208
	title = CHI.lategame.208.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.208.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_sun_fo_gesturing

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus CHI_third_national_congress
	timeout_days = 7

	option = { #In defence of constitutionalism!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.208 option CHI.lategame.208.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.208.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_liberals_march_tt
		if = {
			limit = { CHI_RF_level_seven_trigger = yes }
			CHI_PAC_mega_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					CHI_RF_level_six_trigger = yes
					CHI_RF_level_five_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_PAC_large_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					CHI_RF_level_four_trigger = yes
					CHI_RF_level_three_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_PAC_medium_effect = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					CHI_RF_level_two_trigger = yes
					CHI_RF_level_one_trigger = yes
				}
			}
			CHI_PAC_small_effect = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Long Shadow
	id = CHI.lategame.209
	title = CHI.lategame.209.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.209.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_CRS_meeting

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus CHI_third_national_congress
	timeout_days = 7

	option = { #Such Buffoonery!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.209 option CHI.lategame.209.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.209.a

		set_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_stab_var = CHI_radicalism_var } #Should be between 0-1
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_stab_var = -0.5 } #Should be between -0.5-0
		add_stability = CHI_rad_stab_var

		#Half of radicalism is distributed across radical factions.
		#If CSP Radicals can contest radicalism, only a quarter goes to CRS. Otherwise, half goes to CRS.
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_pop_var = CHI_radicalism_var } #Should be between 0-1
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_RAD_dom_flag }
			multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_pop_var = 0.25 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = CHI_rad_pop_var }
			add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = CHI_rad_pop_var }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_long_shadow_csp_tt
		}
		else = {
			multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_rad_pop_var = 0.50 }
			add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = CHI_rad_pop_var }
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_long_shadow_tt
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Impeachment Vote
	id = CHI.lategame.210
	title = CHI.lategame.210.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.210.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_song_qingling_speech_party_conference_2

	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus CHI_third_national_congress
	timeout_days = 7

	option = { #The die is cast...
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.210 option CHI.lategame.210.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.210.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_impeachment_tt
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = CHI_path option = DEFAULT } #NOT HAVING THE DEFAULT GAMERULE RIGS THE OUTCOME OF THE GAME FOR THE AI
					is_ai = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						var = CHI_radicalism_var
						value = power_balance_value
						compare = greater_than_or_equals
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.350 days = 1 } } #Chaos on the Convention Floor
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CHI_PAC_winning_trigger = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.300 days = 1 } } #Wang is ousted from power!
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CHI_RCA_winning_trigger = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.250 days = 1 } } #Wang Carries the Day!
			}
			else = {
				#fallback
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.350 days = 1 } } #Chaos on the Convention Floor
			}
		}
		else = {
			#Cheaty, cheaty gamerules
			if = {
				limit = {
					CHI_gamerule_scenario_3 = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.350 days = 1 } } #Chaos on the Convention Floor
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CHI_gamerule_song_victory = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.300 days = 1 } } #Wang is ousted from power!
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					CHI_gamerule_wang_victory = yes
				}
				hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.250 days = 1 } } #Wang Carries the Day!
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_power_balance = { id = CHI_power_balance }
		}
	}
}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				china_is_aligned_with_republicans = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_is_aligned_with_left_kmt = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { character = SHX_feng_yuxiang } #RCA more relevant in SHX
					has_country_leader = { character = SZC_lu_chao } #Minor RCA ties

				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { character = YUN_zhu_de } #Has ties with both Political Department and PAC
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_wang_victory = yes
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = { CHI = { CHI_RCA_large_effect = yes } }

			base = 30

				factor = 1.5
				china_is_aligned_with_republicans = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_is_aligned_with_kmt = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_is_aligned_with_left_kmt = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				OR = {
					has_country_leader = { character = GXC_chen_mingshu } #Has ties with PAC
					has_country_leader = { character = YUN_zhu_de } #Has ties with both Political Department and PAC
					has_country_leader = { character = HNN_cheng_qian } #Has ties with RF
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_song_victory = yes
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = { CHI = { CHI_PAC_large_effect = yes } }
		hidden_effect = { CHI = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.213 days = 1 random_days = 6 } } } #[FROM.GetAdjectiveCap] Delegates Align with the Opposition
	}
	option = { #We serve no one but ourselves!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.211 option CHI.lategame.211.c"
		name = CHI.lategame.211.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40

				factor = 1.5

			}

			}

	}

country_event = { #The Republic of China Expels the MMIC
	id = CHI.lategame.220

##Scenario 1: Wang carries the day (250-299)
country_event = { #Wang carries the Day
	id = CHI.lategame.250
	title = CHI.lategame.250.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.250.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_wang_jingwei_mad
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes #triggered from CHI.lategame.210, from 3rd National Congress
	timeout_days = 7

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.251 days = 3 } #Assault on Wuhan
			if = {
				limit = { UPC = { is_subject_of = CHI } }
				UPC = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.291 days = 1 } } #A Rebellion Flares in Fujian!
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RKT = { is_subject_of = CHI } }
				RKT = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.293 days = 1 } } #Rebellion Breaks Out in Fujian!
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.250 option CHI.lategame.250.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.250.a
		activate_advisor = CHI_chen_gongbo_sic
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_soc_dem_stab_loss_tt
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_party_pop_stab_loss_temp_var = party_popularity@social_democrat }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_party_pop_stab_loss_temp_var = -0.5 }
		add_stability = CHI_party_pop_stab_loss_temp_var
		CHI_purge_PAC_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_PAC_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_RF_generals_effect = yes
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 7

		name = CHI.lategame.300.a

			character = CHI_song_qingling
			ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
		}
		activate_advisor = CHI_deng_yanda_sic
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = party_popularity@social_democrat }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = 0.75 }
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = -1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = CHI_neg_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = CHI_pac_party_long
				name = CHI_pac_party
			}
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.301 days = 3 } #The Rising Backlash

				limit = { UPC = { is_subject_of = CHI } }

country_event = {
	id = CHI.lategame.354 #The Lesser Sun
	title = CHI.lategame.354.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.354.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_sun_fo_heroic
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 7

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { UPC = { is_subject_of = CHI } }
				UPC = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.391 days = 3 random_days = 4 } } #The End of the Kuomintang-Federalist Alliance
			}
			if = {
				limit = { RKT = { is_subject_of = CHI } }
				RKT = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.393 days = 3 random_days = 4 } } #The Fallout of the Third Congress
			}
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_tag_in_china_area = yes

						#Only large non-Chinese subjects can influence CHI politics
						strength_ratio = { tag = CHI ratio > 0.5 }
						naval_strength_ratio = { tag = CHI ratio > 1 }
						ic_ratio = { tag = CHI ratio > 0.5 }
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.360 days = 10 } #The Kuomintang Civil War
			}
			if = {
				limit = { CHI = { has_character = CHI_MMIC_theorist } }
				INT = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.365 days = 7 } } #Civil War Breaks Out in China
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.354 option CHI.lategame.354.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.354.a #Begin Negotiations with the PAC
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				check_variable = { CHI_gov_civ_war_var > CHI_crs_civ_war_var }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CHI_pac_won_civil_war_trigger = yes #In this case "winning" not won
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_song_victory = yes
			}
		}
		CHI_recruit_RF_generals_effect = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = syndicalist popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.04 }
		CHI_gov_civ_war_add_3_effect = yes
		CHI_pac_civ_war_add_3_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.370 days = 3 } #The Garrison at Wuhan
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.375 days = 15 } #Battles Along the Coastline
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.376 days = 30 } #Unrest in Nanjing
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.390 days = 40 } #The Dust Settles
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.354 option CHI.lategame.354.b"
		name = CHI.lategame.354.b #Declare Martial Law
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				check_variable = { CHI_crs_civ_war_var > CHI_gov_civ_war_var }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CHI_crs_won_civil_war_trigger = yes #In this case "winning" not won
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_scenario_3 = yes
			}
		}
		CHI_recruit_RF_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_CRS_generals_effect = yes
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.10 }
		CHI_crs_civ_war_add_3_effect = yes
		CHI_rca_civ_war_add_3_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.380 days = 1 } #Special Provisions
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.385 days = 15 } #Mutiny on the High Seas
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.386 days = 30 } #The Push Along the Yangtze
			country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.390 days = 40 } #The Dust Settles!
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 7

	trigger = { NOT = { tag = UPC tag = RKT } } #They get their own revolt if they exist and are a subject of CHI (see CHI.lategame.391)

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.360 option CHI.lategame.360.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.360.a #Side with the PAC
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_is_aligned_with_left_kmt = yes
			}
			modifier = {

			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_song_victory = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.361 days = 3 random_days = 7 } } }

			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_is_aligned_with_left_kmt = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_chen_victory = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.362 days = 3 random_days = 7 } } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.360 option CHI.lategame.360.c"
		name = CHI.lategame.360.c #Side with the Government
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_country_leader = { character = HNN_cheng_qian }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				china_is_aligned_with_right_kmt = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				china_is_aligned_with_federalists = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.363 days = 3 random_days = 7 } } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.360 option CHI.lategame.360.e"
		name = CHI.lategame.360.e #It is time we broke free
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_chinese_tag = yes
				china_is_aligned_with_republicans = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				is_chinese_tag = yes
				china_is_aligned_with_kmt = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = CHI
					ratio > 0.80
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = CHI
					ratio > 0.8
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				CHI = { has_war = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_chinese_tag = no
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = CHI
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000
				CHI_gamerule_hu_victory = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { FROM = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.364 days = 3 random_days = 7 } } }
		create_wargoal = {
			target = FROM
			type = topple_government
		}
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_chinese_tag = yes }
				china_break_puppet_effect = yes
			}
			else = {
				leave_faction = yes
				overlord = {
					set_temp_variable = { former_overlord = THIS }
					set_autonomy = {
						target = PREV
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
				peace_out_non_neighbours_after_leaving_faction = yes
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_china = yes
						NOT = { is_core_of = var:former_overlord }
					}
					add_claim_by = var:former_overlord
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				create_wargoal = {
					target = ROOT
					type = annex_everything
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_riot3

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.376 option CHI.lategame.376.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.376.a #He reaches his bunker safely...
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = CHI_gov_civ_war_var
				value = CHI_crs_civ_war_var
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var = CHI_pac_civ_war_var }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var
			min = 1 #It will always boost a faction
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_gov_civ_war_var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var }
		set_variable = { CHI_crs_civ_war_var = 0 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_nanjing_unrest_gov_victory_tt
	}

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.376 option CHI.lategame.376.b"

		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = CHI_crs_civ_war_var
				value = CHI_gov_civ_war_var
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var = CHI_gov_civ_war_var }
		clamp_temp_variable = {
			var = CHI_nanjing_boost_temp_var
			min = 1 #It will always boost a faction
		}
		add_to_variable = { CHI_crs_civ_war_var = CHI_gov_civ_war_var }
		set_variable = { CHI_gov_civ_war_var = 0 }
		CHI_hu_zongnan = { promote_character = totalist_subtype }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_nanjing_unrest_crs_takeover_tt
	}
}

#Chinese Civil War Conclusion Chain

country_event = {
	id = CHI.lategame.390 #The Dust Settles!
	title = CHI.lategame.390.t
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.390.d.GOV
		trigger = { CHI_gov_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.390.d.CRS
		trigger = { CHI_crs_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.390.d.RCA
		trigger = { CHI_rca_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }
	}
	desc = {
		text = CHI.lategame.390.d.PAC #Default Winner
		trigger = { CHI_pac_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_intelligence
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	timeout_days = 7

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = CHI_civil_war_over_flag } }

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.390 option CHI.lategame.390.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.390.a #Song Qingling's government prevails
		trigger = { CHI_gov_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }

		#Set Up Politics
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = CHI_song_qingling
			ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
		}
		activate_advisor = CHI_sun_fo_sic
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = party_popularity@social_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = -0.75 } #We're gonna subtract about 75% of soc dem popularity
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_add_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_add_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = 0.50 } #About 50% of Soc Dem Popularity will turn into Rad Soc
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_add_soc_lib_popularity_temp_var = CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_add_soc_lib_popularity_temp_var = 0.25 } #About 25% of Soc Dem Popularity will turn into Soc Lib
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = CHI_neg_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = CHI_add_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = CHI_add_soc_lib_popularity_temp_var }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = CHI_revolutionary_committee_party_long
				name = CHI_revolutionary_committee_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = CHI_rca_moderate_party_long
				name = CHI_rca_moderate_party
			}
		}

		#Fallback to ensure characters work okay
		CHI_recruit_PAC_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_RF_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_PAC_endgame_advisors_effect = yes
		activate_advisor = CHI_sun_fo_sic
		CHI_purge_RCA_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_RCA_generals_effect = yes
		#CRS, RF, and LCS Generals/Advisors Purged later in content

		#Setup Focus Tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = no }
			complete_national_focus = CHI_action_now
		}

	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.390 option CHI.lategame.390.b"
		name = CHI.lategame.390.b #Deng Yanda wipes out the traitors!
		trigger = { CHI_pac_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }

		#Set Up Politics
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = CHI_song_qingling
			ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = party_popularity@social_democrat }
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_neg_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = -0.60 } #We're gonna subtract about 75% of soc dem popularity
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_add_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = CHI_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_add_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var = 0.60 } #About 50% of Soc Dem Popularity will turn into Rad Soc
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = CHI_neg_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = CHI_add_soc_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = CHI_revolutionary_committee_party_long
				name = CHI_revolutionary_committee_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				long_name = CHI_rca_moderate_party_long
				name = CHI_rca_moderate_party
			}
		}

		#Fallback to ensure everything works properly character-wise
		CHI_recruit_PAC_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_PAC_endgame_advisors_effect = yes
		activate_advisor = CHI_deng_yanda_sic
		#CRS, RF, and LCS Generals/Advisors Purged later in content

		#Set Up Focus Tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = no }
			complete_national_focus = CHI_action_now
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.390 option CHI.lategame.390.c"
		name = CHI.lategame.390.c #Hu Zongnan triumphs over all!
		trigger = { CHI_crs_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = totalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		CHI_hu_zongnan = { promote_character = totalist_subtype }
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_dai_chunfeng = { promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
			CHI_lixingshe = { promote_character = paternal_autocrat_subtype }
		}
		activate_advisor = CHI_lixingshe_sic
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = 0.20 }

		#Fallback to ensure everything works properly character-wise
		CHI_recruit_CRS_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_CRS_endgame_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_RF_generals_effect = yes

		CHI_purge_CSP_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_RCA_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_PAC_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_PAC_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_LCS_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_RCA_generals_effect = yes

		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = no }
			complete_national_focus = CHI_the_second_national_revolution
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.390 option CHI.lategame.390.d"
		name = CHI.lategame.390.d #Chen Gongbo emerges victorious!
		trigger = { CHI_rca_won_civil_war_trigger = yes }

		#Set Up Politics
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		promote_character = {
			character = CHI_zeng_zhongming
			ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				long_name = CHI_rca_radical_party_long
				name = CHI_rca_radical_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = syndicalist
				long_name = CHI_csp_ort_party_long
				name = CHI_csp_ort_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = totalist
				long_name = CHI_csp_rad_party_long
				name = CHI_csp_rad_party
			}
			CHI_chen_shaoyu = { promote_character = totalist_subtype }
		}

		#Fallback to ensure characters work okay
		CHI_recruit_RCA_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_recruit_RCA_endgame_advisors_effect = yes
		activate_advisor = CHI_chen_gongbo_sic
		CHI_purge_PAC_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_PAC_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_RF_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_CRS_advisors_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_CRS_generals_effect = yes

		#Setup Focus Tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = no }
			complete_national_focus = CHI_the_second_reorganisation
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #A Republican Alliance?
	id = CHI.lategame.901
	title = CHI.lategame.901.t
	desc = CHI.lategame.901.d

	picture = GFX_report_event_YUN_KMT
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by decision CHI_subjugate_federalists_decision
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_war_with = CHI }
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.901 option CHI.lategame.901.a"
		name = CHI.lategame.901.a #For our nation and its republic, we reluctantly accept.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.75
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If CHI dwarfs Federalist industry
				factor = 3
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
			}
			modifier = { #If FNG/MAN has turtled up by joining Co-Pro - Patriotic Fevor. Only applies if CHI can actually beat them though
				factor = 5
				var:716.owner = {
					is_ally_with = JAP
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = FROM
						ratio < 1
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				CHI = { CHI_gu_mengyu = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_will_be_subjugated_tt
		effect_tooltip = { FROM = { china_puppet_ROOT_effect = yes } }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = FROM decision = CHI_betrayal_decision }
		set_country_flag = { flag = CHI_compromise_subjugation_timer_flag days = 180 value = 1 } # Value needs to be there or the effect won't work
		if = {
			limit = { CHI = { CHI_gu_mengyu = { is_second_in_command = yes } } }
			add_political_power = 25
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -75
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.902 days = 3 } } #A Renewed Republican Alliance
			every_subject_country = {
				country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.904 days = 7 random_days = 7 } #Chen Submits to Nanjing
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.lategame.901 option CHI.lategame.901.b"
		name = CHI.lategame.901.b #For the good of freedom and democracy, we must decline!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 70
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.3
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure Military Strength
				factor = 3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 2
				}
			}
			modifier = { #Measure # of Fed Puppets
				factor = 3
				num_subjects > 2
			}
			modifier = { #Measure # of Fed Puppets
				factor = 5
				num_subjects > 4
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = CHI_ally_betrayal option = CHI_ALLY_BETRAYAL_NEVER }
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = FROM
			modifier = KR_outraged
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10
		FROM = { hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = CHI.lategame.903 days = 3 } } } #Federalist Talks Reach an Impasse!
	}
}

					ratio > 2
				}

			limit = { NOT = { has_template = "Liberation Army Division" } }

				name = "Liberation Army Division"
				division_names_group = CHI_MIL_01
				is_locked = yes
				force_allow_recruiting = yes
				template_counter = 58
				regiments = {
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 1 y = 2 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 0 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 1 }
					infantry = { x = 2 y = 2 }
				}
				support = {
					artillery = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					rangers = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					recon = { x = 0 y = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		set_division_template_lock = {
			division_template = "Liberation Army Division"
			is_locked = no
		}
		clear_division_template_cap = {
			division_template = "Liberation Army Division"
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = CHI.endgame.261 #The Expanded Party Conference
	title = CHI.endgame.261.t
	desc = CHI.endgame.261.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_1948_presidential_election
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_sun_fo = {
				CHI_recruit_character_effect = yes
				promote_character = social_liberal_subtype
			}
			CHI_assorted_leaders = {
				promote_character = market_liberal_subtype
				promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
				promote_character = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
				promote_character = paternal_autocrat_subtype
				promote_character = national_populist_subtype
			}

			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.asian_tags_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_tag_in_china_area = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								tag = UPC
								tag = CHI
							}
						}
						event_target:CHI_UPC_compromise_Fed_leader = {
							remove_second_in_command_role = yes
							CHI_recruit_character_effect = yes
							add_country_leader_role = {
								country_leader = { ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
								promote_leader = yes
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								exists = no
								tag = CHI
								NOT = { has_character = GXC_zhang_junmai } #Check to see if he's been retired
							}
						}
						GXC_zhang_junmai = {
							remove_second_in_command_role = yes
							CHI_recruit_character_effect = yes
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
								promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									country_leader = { ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
									promote_leader = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								exists = no
								tag = CHI
								NOT = { has_character = GXC_li_zongren } #Check to see if he's been retired
							}
						}
						GXC_li_zongren = {
							CHI_recruit_li_zongren_effect = yes
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype }
								promote_character = paternal_autocrat_subtype
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									country_leader = { ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype }
									promote_leader = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								exists = no
								tag = CHI
								NOT = { has_character = SHX_feng_yuxiang } #Check to see if he's been retired
							}
						}
						SHX_feng_yuxiang = {
							remove_second_in_command_role = yes
							CHI_recruit_character_effect = yes
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = national_populist_subtype }
								promote_character = national_populist_subtype
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									country_leader = { ideology = national_populist_subtype }
									promote_leader = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}

			set_party_name = { ideology = market_liberal name = CHI_PIP_party long_name = CHI_PIP_party_long }
			set_party_name = { ideology = social_conservative name = CHI_CDL_party long_name = CHI_CDL_party_long }
			set_party_name = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat name = CHI_market_liberal_party long_name = CHI_market_liberal_party_long }
			set_party_name = { ideology = paternal_autocrat name = CHI_rkmt_party long_name = CHI_rkmt_party_long }
			set_party_name = { ideology = national_populist name = CHI_gmj_party long_name = CHI_gmj_party_long }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.endgame.261 option CHI.endgame.261.a"
		name = CHI.endgame.261.a

		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.04 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.04 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.02 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.02 }
	}
}

country_event = { #The Party and the People
	id = CHI.endgame.402
	title = CHI.endgame.402.t
	desc = CHI.endgame.402.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_labour_rally
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.endgame.402 option CHI.endgame.402.a"
		name = CHI.endgame.402.a
		add_ideas = CHI_popular_protests_idea
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = CHI_LCS_RAD_dom_flag }
			CHI_LCS_clear_flags_effect = yes
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { CHI_WRD_SOC_strength_var > CHI_CSP_ORT_strength_var } }
				set_country_flag = CHI_LCS_WRD_dom_flag
				promote_character = {
					character = CHI_yi_peiji
					ideology = syndicalist_subtype
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = syndicalist
						name = CHI_wrd_soc_party
						long_name = CHI_wrd_soc_party_long
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = CHI_LCS_ORT_dom_flag
				promote_character = {
					character = CHI_chen_duxiu
					ideology = syndicalist_subtype
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = syndicalist
						name = CHI_csp_ort_party
						long_name = CHI_csp_ort_party_long
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = CHI.endgame.403 days = 3 } #Hardliners and Compromisers
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The Liberal Ironneck
	id = CHI.endgame.404
	title = CHI.endgame.404.t
	desc = CHI.endgame.404.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_sun_fo_bitch_please
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes #Fired from focus CHI_promises_of_democracy

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.endgame.404 option CHI.endgame.404.a"
		name = CHI.endgame.404.a #A tough, but fair bargain.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				social_liberal > 0.20
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					CHI_sun_fo = { is_political_advisor = yes }
					CHI_sun_fo = { is_second_in_command = yes }
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_sun_fo_is_helpful_tt
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = -0.10
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.10
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = CHI_sun_fo_helpful_tt
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.endgame.404 option CHI.endgame.404.b"
		name = CHI.endgame.404.b #Let’s see how tough he truly is.
		trigger = {
			NOT = { CHI_sun_fo = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				syndicalist > 0.20
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = -0.05 }
		CHI_exile_sun_fo_effect = yes
		effect_tooltip = { CHI_sun_fo = { retire = yes } }
	}
}

	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.endgame.407 option CHI.endgame.407.b"
		name = CHI.endgame.407.b #Sideline Hu Zongnan’s Clique
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { stability > party_popularity@totalist }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				totalist < 0.10
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_totalist_pop_temp_var = party_popularity@totalist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_totalist_pop_temp_var = -0.5 }
		add_stability = CHI_totalist_pop_temp_var
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = CHI_totalist_pop_temp_var }
		CHI_purge_CRS_generals_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			promote_character = {
				character = CHI_dai_chunfeng
				ideology = totalist_subtype
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.endgame.407 option CHI.endgame.407.c"
		name = CHI.endgame.407.c #Purge them once and for all!
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { stability > party_popularity@totalist }
			totalist < 0.15
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				totalist < 0.05
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { CHI_totalist_pop_temp_var = party_popularity@totalist }
		multiply_temp_variable = { CHI_totalist_pop_temp_var = -1 }
		add_stability = CHI_totalist_pop_temp_var
		add_popularity = { ideology = totalist popularity = CHI_totalist_pop_temp_var }
		CHI_purge_CRS_generals_effect = yes
		CHI_purge_CRS_advisors_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {

				character = CHI_lixingshe
				ideology = totalist_subtype
			}

		}

country_event = { #The United Front Work Department
	id = CHI.endgame.441
	title = CHI.endgame.441.t
	desc = CHI.endgame.441.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_zhang_junmai
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			CHI_assorted_leaders = {
				promote_character = { ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
				promote_character = { ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
				promote_character = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype }
			}
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = global.asian_tags_array
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_tag_in_china_area = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								exists = no
								tag = CHI
								NOT = { has_character = GXC_zhang_junmai } #Check to see if he's been retired
							}
						}
						GXC_zhang_junmai = {
							remove_second_in_command_role = yes
							CHI_recruit_character_effect = yes
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
								promote_character = market_liberal_subtype
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									country_leader = { ideology = market_liberal_subtype }
									promote_leader = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							OR = {
								exists = no
								tag = CHI
								NOT = { has_character = QIE_james_yen } #Check to see if he's been retired
							}
						}
						QIE_james_yen = {
							remove_second_in_command_role = yes
							CHI_recruit_character_effect = yes
							if = {
								limit = { has_ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
								promote_character = social_conservative_subtype
							}
							else = {
								add_country_leader_role = {
									country_leader = { ideology = social_conservative_subtype }
									promote_leader = yes
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = CHI_CDL_party_long
				name = CHI_CDL_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = CHI_RRA_party_long
				name = CHI_RRA_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = CHI_market_liberal_party_long
				name = CHI_market_liberal_party
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #We welcome them cordially.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.endgame.441 option CHI.endgame.441.a"
		name = CHI.endgame.441.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				social_liberal > 0.25
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.075 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.075 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.10 }
	}
	option = { #Keep an eye on their activities.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event CHI.endgame.441 option CHI.endgame.441.b"
		name = CHI.endgame.441.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				radical_socialist < 0.25
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.07 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.025 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.025 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.03 }
	}
}
